#Doppeldenken - Speer's reign of contrast begins.
shared_focus = {
	id = SGR_doppeldenken
	icon = GFX_focus_GER_doppeldenken
	cost = 1.00
	x = 0
	y = 0

	allow_branch = {
		NOT = { has_global_flag = SGR_natsoc_collapse }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = SGR_phase2 }
		has_global_flag = german_civil_war_speervic
	}

	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus SGR_doppeldenken"
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = speer.10004
				days = 130
				random_hours = 60
			}
			country_event = {
				id = speer.10000
				days = 14
			}
			country_event = {
				id = speerflavor.104
				days = 4
			}
		}
		TNO_improve_political_parties_policy_effectiveness_low = yes
	}
}

#In the Halls of Germania - the Gang of Four begins its energetic work in Germania's offices, planning for the future to come.
shared_focus = {
	id = SGR_in_the_halls_of_germania
	icon = GFX_focus_GER_in_the_halls_of_germania
	cost = 1.00
	prerequisite = {
		focus = SGR_doppeldenken
	}
	relative_position_id = SGR_doppeldenken
	x = -1
	y = 1


	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus SGR_in_the_halls_of_germania"
		add_political_power = 30
		custom_effect_tooltip = SGR_gang_of_four_work_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = speerflavor.32
				days = 17
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = paternalism
			popularity = 0.02
		}
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		base = 20
		modifier = {
			NOT = { check_variable = { TNO_Espionage_Agency = token:Espionage_RND } }
			factor = 50
		}
	}
}

#End Aryan Lineage Studies - The Ahnenpass will be abolished, once and for all.
shared_focus = {
	id = SGR_end_aryan_lineage_studies
	icon = GFX_focus_GER_end_aryan_lineage_studies
	cost = 2.00
	prerequisite = {
		focus = SGR_deny_our_complicity
	}
	prerequisite = {
		focus = SGR_show_their_crimes
	}
	prerequisite = {
		focus = SGR_to_all_who_fought
	}
	prerequisite = {
		focus = SGR_to_all_who_worked
	}
	prerequisite = {
		focus = SGR_open_the_ports
	}
	mutually_exclusive = {
		focus = SGR_suspend_the_persecution
	}
	relative_position_id = SGR_to_all_who_fought
	x = 0
	y = 1



	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus SGR_end_aryan_lineage_studies"
		add_political_power = -50
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = national_socialism
			popularity = -0.02
		}
		increase_reformist_leaning_medium = yes
		decrease_regime_stab_med = yes
		TNO_improve_education_policy_effectiveness_low = yes
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		base = 15
		modifier = {
			NOT = { check_variable = { TNO_Espionage_Agency = token:Espionage_RND } }
			factor = 50
		}
	}
}

#Open the Ports - the Reich must trade with the outside world to sustain itself in these trying times.
shared_focus = {
	id = SGR_open_the_ports
	icon = GFX_focus_GER_open_the_ports
	cost = 1.00
	prerequisite = {
		focus = SGR_aid_for_the_present
	}
	relative_position_id = SGR_aid_for_the_present
	x = 0
	y = 1



	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus SGR_open_the_ports"
		set_temp_variable = { gdp_growth_temp = 0.75 }
		econ_gdp_growth_change = yes
		TNO_improve_trade_laws_policy_effectiveness_low = yes
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_idea = tno_trade_laws_limited_exports } }
			add_ideas = tno_trade_laws_limited_exports
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			SGR_deficit_offset = 0.05
		}
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		base = 20
		modifier = {
			NOT = { check_variable = { TNO_Espionage_Agency = token:Espionage_RND } }
			factor = 50
		}
	}
}

#Review the Laws - The Nuremberg Laws will be reviewed, with Speer promising leniency.
shared_focus = {
	id = SGR_review_the_laws
	icon = GFX_focus_GER_review_the_laws
	cost = 1.00
	prerequisite = {
		focus = SGR_end_aryan_lineage_studies
		focus = SGR_suspend_the_persecution
	}
	relative_position_id = SGR_suspend_the_persecution
	x = -2
	y = 1



	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus SGR_review_the_laws"
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = SGR_end_aryan_lineage_studies
			}
			add_political_power = 50
			else = {
				add_political_power = 20
			}
		}
		add_stability = 0.025
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		base = 20
		modifier = {
			NOT = { check_variable = { TNO_Espionage_Agency = token:Espionage_RND } }
			factor = 50
		}
	}
}

#Revitalizing Science - A large batch of investment into the Kaiser-Wilhelms-Gesellschaft, Fraunhofer Institut and other renomated German scientific agencies,
shared_focus = {
	id = SGR_revitalizing_science
	icon = GFX_focus_GER_revitalizing_science
	cost = 1.00
	prerequisite = {
		focus = SGR_ausbildung_initiative
		focus = SGR_wehrmacht_engineering_schools
	}
	relative_position_id = SGR_wehrmacht_engineering_schools
	x = 1
	y = 1



	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus SGR_revitalizing_science"
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = SGR_ausbildung_initiative
			}
			set_temp_variable = { temp_econ_spending_amount = 0.45 }
			econ_spend_money_once_effect_raw_money = yes
			add_ideas = GER_SGR_scientific_investment
			TNO_improve_academic_base_high = yes
			TNO_improve_research_facilities_med = yes
			else = {
				set_temp_variable = { temp_econ_spending_amount = 0.25 }
				econ_spend_money_once_effect_raw_money = yes
				add_ideas = GER_SGR_scientific_investment
				TNO_improve_academic_base_med = yes
				TNO_improve_research_facilities_low = yes
			}
		}
	}
	ai_will_do = {

shared_focus = {
	id = GER_the_mad_count
	icon = GFX_focus_GER_the_mad_count

	allow_branch = {
		NOT = { has_country_flag = SGR_phase2 }
		has_country_flag = SGR_CAU_tree2
	}

	x = 23
	y = 7

	cost = 1

	will_lead_to_war_with = CAU
	will_lead_to_war_with = AZR
	will_lead_to_war_with = GEO
	will_lead_to_war_with = ADY
	will_lead_to_war_with = DAG

	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus GER_the_mad_count"
		declare_war_on = {
			target = CAU
			type = annex_everything
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { country_exists = AZR }
				declare_war_on = {
					target = AZR
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { country_exists = GEO }
				declare_war_on = {
					target = GEO
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { country_exists = ADY }
				declare_war_on = {
					target = ADY
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { country_exists = DAG }
				declare_war_on = {
					target = DAG
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

shared_focus = {
	id = GER_funky_fresh_speerscience
	icon = GFX_focus_GER_new_science

	cost = 3

	x = 30
	y = 0

	allow_branch = {
		NOT = { has_global_flag = SGR_natsoc_collapse }
		has_country_flag = SGR_phase2
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = SGR_phase3
		}
	}
	available = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_ai = no
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = SGR_research_expenditure_above_70
				check_variable = { econ_research_expenditures_slider_pct > 69 }
			}
		}
	}

	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus GER_funky_fresh_speerscience"
		random_list = {
			40 = {
				add_tech_bonus = {
					name = industry
					bonus = 0.50
					uses = 1
					category = industry
				}
			}
			40 = {
				add_tech_bonus = {
					name = construction_tech
					bonus = 0.50
					uses = 1
					category = construction_tech
				}
			}
			20 = {
				add_research_slot = 1
				hidden_effect = {
					country_event = {
						id = speerscience.4
						days = 100
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = SGR_science_temp_res_slot
			}
		}
		country_event = {
			id = speerscience.3
		}
	}
}

#Achilles' Heel, Struck - The Oil Crisis begins, launching Germany into its worst economic regression since the BÃ¼rgerkrieg.
shared_focus = {
	id = GER_achilles_heel_struck
	icon = GFX_focus_GER_oil_crisis_struck
	cost = 3.00
	x = 30
	y = 0

	allow_branch = {
		NOT = { has_global_flag = SGR_natsoc_collapse }
		has_global_flag = german_civil_war_speervic
		has_country_flag = SGR_phase3
		has_idea = SGR_OC_protests
	}
	bypass = {
		has_country_flag = SGR_phase3

	id = SGR_memories_of_autarky
	icon = GFX_focus_GER_industrial_revitalization
	cost = 2.00

	prerequisite = {
		focus = SGR_energiesicherungsgesetz
	}

	mutually_exclusive = {
		focus = SGR_open_ports
	}

	relative_position_id = SGR_energiesicherungsgesetz
	x = 2
	y = 1

	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus SGR_memories_of_autarky"
		tno_trade_laws_improve = yes
		add_regime_stab_small = yes
		set_variable = { tno_trade_laws_effectiveness = 90 }
		TNO_improve_trade_laws_policy_effectiveness_monthly_med = yes
	}
}

			has_country_flag = SGR_SR_fash_outcome
			has_country_flag = SGR_SR_authdem_outcome
		}
	}

	prerequisite = {
		focus = SGR_reichsschutzgruppe
	}

		focus = SGR_the_plan_going_forward
	}

		focus = SGR_freiheit
		focus = SGR_ein_fuhrer
	}

	x = 4
	y = 1

			id = speerphase3.11
			days = 2
		}

			limit = {
				NOT = { has_idea = tno_trade_laws_free_trade }

		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus SGR_collect_the_proposals"
		add_political_power = 50
	}
}

#Koalition der Nationen - the letters have been drafted and are being sent out into the world.
shared_focus = {
	id = SGR_koalition_der_nationen
	icon = GFX_focus_GER_koalition_der_nationen
	cost = 3.00

	prerequisite = {
		focus = SGR_collect_the_proposals
	}
	prerequisite = {
		focus = SGR_prime_the_ambassadors
	}


	relative_position_id = SGR_prime_the_ambassadors
	x = 1
	y = 2

	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus SGR_koalition_der_nationen"
		custom_effect_tooltip = SGR_KN_focus_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			JAP = {
				country_event = {
					id = speerphase3.14
					days = 2
				}
			}
			USA = {
				country_event = {
					id = speerphase3.14
					days = 2
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = SGR_ein_fuhrer
				}
				country_event = {
					id = speerphase3.15
					days = 4
				}
				else = {
					country_event = {
						id = speerphase3.16
						days = 4
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# enjoyed a small peak into a world that, whilst dark and looming, still has some glimmers of hope that may grow into a fire. Thank you so much for playing, and we hope you'll come back for the rest
# of Speer's and the Gang of Four's story in TNO2!
